#### Switzerland
############
event = {
	id = 996000
	tag = { RUS SOV FRA CSA ENG HUN AUS U24 U25 ITA RSI VIC U08 U07 U23 USA TEX U31 U14 }
	style = 2
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		NOT = {
			exists = SCH
			local_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 389 data = -1 } #Zurich
		control = { province = 390 data = -1 } #Lugano
		control = { province = 391 data = -1 } #Geneva
		control = { province = 392 data = -1 } #Bern
	}

	decision_trigger = { }

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			exists = SCH
			local_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 389 data = -1 } #Zurich
		control = { province = 390 data = -1 } #Lugano
		control = { province = 391 data = -1 } #Geneva
		control = { province = 392 data = -1 } #Bern
	}

	name = "The Annexation of Switzerland"
	desc = "After fierce fighting in the Alpine Mountains, we have conquered and annexed Switzerland. The Swiss army has surrendered, and the territory is under our control, but the people are still resistant."
	picture = "militaryparade1"
	decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 1 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 1
		name = "Hurrah!"
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SWITZ_CONQ }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 99
		name = "Liberate a friendly Switzerland!"
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { type = independence which = SCH value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = SCH }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 996001
	tag = { ROM GRE SER OTT AUS U24 U25 HUN GER ITA RUS SOV FRA RSI ENG TEX CSA JAP U31 YUG USA U07 U08 }
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		NOT = {
			exists = BUL
			local_flag = BUL_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 321 data = -1 } #Sofia
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = -1 country = TUR }
			war = { country = -1 country = OTT }
			war = { country = -1 country = ROM }
			war = { country = -1 country = URU }
			war = { country = -1 country = GRE }
			war = { country = -1 country = SER }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = -1 country = TUR }
			war = { country = -1 country = OTT }
			war = { country = -1 country = ROM }
			war = { country = -1 country = URU }
			war = { country = -1 country = GRE }
			war = { country = -1 country = SER }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
			exists = BUL
			local_flag = BUL_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 321 data = -1 } #Sofia
	}

	name = "The Annexation of Bulgaria"
	desc = "After a long fight with the Bulgarian Empire, we have launched a full offensive and forced the Bulgarian Army to surrender. Sofia is now in our hands!"

	decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = 0 year = 1964 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 1
		name = "Occupy them, for now..."

		command = { trigger = { country = SER } type = addcore which = 331 } #Pirot

		command = { trigger = { country = SER } type = addcore which = 334 } #Tetovo

		command = { trigger = { country = OTT } type = addcore which = 325 }
		command = { trigger = { country = OTT } type = addclaim which = 324 }
		command = { trigger = { country = OTT } type = addclaim which = 319 }
		command = { trigger = { country = OTT } type = addclaim which = 363 }
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = BUL_CONQ }
	}
	action = {

		name = "Liberate a friendly Bulgaria!"
		trigger = { NOT = { country = SER } }
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { trigger = { country = OTT } type = addcore which = 370 }

event = {
	id = 996003
	tag = { GRE SER OTT AUS U24 U25 HUN GER ITA RUS SOV FRA RSI ENG U31 CSA TEX JAP BUL POL U00 }
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country = BUL }
			government = { type = communist country = BUL }
		}
		NOT = {
			exists = ROM
			exists = URU
			local_flag = ROM_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 316 data = -1 } #Bucharest
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = -1 country = UKR }
			war = { country = -1 country = U24 }
			war = { country = -1 country = U25 }
			war = { country = -1 country = HUN }
			war = { country = -1 country = BUL }
			war = { country = -1 country = SER }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country = BUL }
			government = { type = communist country = BUL }
		}
		control = { province = 316 data = -1 } #Bucharest
		NOT = {
			exists = ROM
			exists = URU
			war = { country = -1 country = UKR }
			war = { country = -1 country = U24 }
			war = { country = -1 country = U25 }
			war = { country = -1 country = HUN }
			war = { country = -1 country = BUL }
			war = { country = -1 country = SER }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
			local_flag = ROM_CONQ
		}
	}

	name = "The Annexation of Romania"
	desc = "The Iron Guard has been extinguished and Romania has been annexed. We no longer have to worry about them."
	picture = "POWs"
	decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 0 month = 0 year = 1936 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = 0 year = 1964 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 1
		name = "Occupy them, for now..."
		command = { type = local_setflag which = ROM_CONQ }
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 99
		name = "Restore independent Romania!"
		command = { trigger = { country = RUS flag = RUS_EXP } type = add_claim_area which = "Bessarabia" }
		command = { trigger = { country = RUS flag = RUS_EXP } type = removeclaim which = 300 }
		command = { trigger = { country = SOV flag = SOV_EXP } type = add_claim_area which = "Bessarabia" }
		command = { trigger = { country = SOV flag = SOV_EXP } type = removeclaim which = 300 }
		command = { type = independence which = URU value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = URU }
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { trigger = { government = communist } type = flag_ext where = URU which = "_syn" }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 996005
	tag = { BUL GRE ROM OTT AUS U24 U25 HUN GER ITA RUS SOV FRA RSI ENG CSA U31 TEX JAP POL U00 }
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country = BUL }
			government = { type = communist country = BUL }
		}
		NOT = {
			exists = SER
			local_flag = SER_CONQ
		}
		control = { province = 338 data = -1 } #Belgrade
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			war = { country = -1 country = U24 }
			war = { country = -1 country = U25 }
			war = { country = -1 country = AUS }
			war = { country = -1 country = HUN }
			war = { country = -1 country = CRO }
			war = { country = -1 country = BOS }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
			war = { country = -1 country = BUL }
			war = { country = -1 country = ALB }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		control = { province = 338 data = -1 } #Belgrade
		OR = {
			NOT = { country = BUL }
			government = { type = communist country = BUL }
		}

		NOT = {
			exists = SER
			war = { country = -1 country = U24 }
			war = { country = -1 country = U25 }
			war = { country = -1 country = AUS }
			war = { country = -1 country = HUN }
			war = { country = -1 country = CRO }
			war = { country = -1 country = BOS }
			war = { country = -1 country = YUG }
			war = { country = -1 country = BUL }
			war = { country = -1 country = ALB }
			local_flag = SER_CONQ
		}
	}

	name = "The Annexation of Serbia"
	desc = "The Serbian State has been annexed, our troops are parading in Belgrade. A major threat to the stability in the region has been removed."
	picture = "POWs"
	decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 0 month = 0 year = 1936 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = 0 year = 1964 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 1
		name = "Hurrah!"
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SER_CONQ }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 99
		name = "Restore friendly Serbia!"
		command = { type = supplies value = 1000 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = independence which = SER value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = SER }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { government = communist } } type = name where = SER which = SER_KIN_NAME }
		command = { type = trigger which = 11800163 }
	}
}

	control = { province = 111 data = -1 } #Arlon

Another possibility is the final separation of Flanders-Wallonia into independent states."

event = {
id = 11800185
tag = { OTT TRA TUR ARM AZB PER KUR RUS SOV USA FRA CSA TEX ARA GER AUS VIC U43 IND PAK PRK }
persistent = yes

decision = {
	control = { province = 709 data = -1 }
	NOT = {
		local_flag = GEO_CONQ
		core = { province = 709 data = -1 }
		exists = GEO
		OR = {
			AND = { country = RUS flag = RUS_EXP }
			AND = { country = SOV flag = SOV_EXP }
		}
	}
}

decision_trigger = { }

trigger = {
	control = { province = 709 data = -1 }
	NOT = {
		local_flag = GEO_CONQ
		core = { province = 709 data = -1 }
		exists = GEO
		OR = {
			AND = { country = RUS flag = RUS_EXP }
			AND = { country = SOV flag = SOV_EXP }
		}
	}

tag = { GER CAN VIC ITA USA TEX CSA RUS SOV U07 U08 U23 U25 U24 FRA ENG U31 RSI U14 } #This restricts the valid targets, speeding up the resolution of the trigger.
all = yes #This combination is dangerous, so use with caution.
persistent = yes
trigger = { local_flag = { which = SPADE_TAK when = 0 value = 1 } }
style = 2
picture = "militaryparade1"

name = "Spanish states under our control"
desc = "The partition of Spain is now complete, as the Madrid-based government has turned control of its former autonomous communities of Galiza, Catalonia and the Basque Country to us."

action = {
	name = "Nice!"
	command = { type = make_puppet which = EUS }
	command = { type = make_puppet which = SPR }
	command = { type = make_puppet which = U37 }
	command = { type = make_puppet which = U37 }
	command = { type = local_setflag which = SPADE_TAK when = 0 value = 2 } # This breaks the infinite loop that all + persistent can cause.
}
}

	control = { province = 163 data = -1 }
	NOT = {
		local_flag = GER_AUSCONQ

	OR = {
		flag = GER_Capitulation
		flag = GER_CON_Capitulation
		NOT = { exists = GER }

	}

event = {
id = 62901
country = ITA
style = 2
picture = "militaryparade1"
decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"
persistent = yes

decision = {
	control = { province = 29 data = -1 } # London
	alliance = { country = EUS country = ITA }
	NOT = {
		government = communist
		exists = SCO
		exists = U16
		alliance = { country = CAN country = -1 }
		alliance = { country = U07 country = -1 }
		alliance = { country = GER country = -1 }
		war = { country = ENG country = -1 }
	}
}

decision_trigger = { }

trigger = {
	control = { province = 29 data = -1 } # London
	OR = {
		alliance = { country = EUS country = -1 }
		alliance = { country = ITA country = -1 }
	}
	NOT = {
		government = communist
		exists = SCO
		exists = U16
		alliance = { country = CAN country = -1 }
		alliance = { country = U07 country = -1 }
		alliance = { country = GER country = -1 }
		war = { country = ENG country = -1 }
	}
}

offset = 15
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }

	ai_chance = 50
	name = "Create a loyal, United Britain"
	trigger = { NOT = { exists = U07 } }
	command = { type = independence which = U07 value = 1 when = 0 }
	command = { type = make_puppet which = U07 }
	command = { type = trigger which = 62902 }
}

	ai_chance = 50
	name = "Independence for England and Scotland"

	war = { country = CAN country = RUS }
	control = { province = 2106 data = RUS } # Winnipeg
	control = { province = 2108 data = RUS } # Ottawa
	control = { province = 2111 data = RUS } # Toronto
	control = { province = 2119 data = RUS } # Montreal
	control = { province = 2126 data = RUS } # Quebec City, to show Russia is clearly advancing
	OR = {
		control = { province = 2132 data = RUS } # Halifax
		control = { province = 2089 data = RUS } # Vancouver
	}
	control = { province = 572 data = RUS } # Moscow, to make sure Russians are in a position to dictate demands
	control = { province = 553 data = RUS } # Petrograd, to make sure Russians are in a position to dictate demands
	NOT = {
		ispuppet = RUS
		ispuppet = CAN
		control = { province = 1832 } # Chicago, to make sure the Canadians are not making heavy advances of their own against the CSA/AUS/PSA
	}
